# 8000 Essential English Words for Senior High School Students

> A comprehensive vocabulary list for non-native senior high school (高中) students in Taiwan, organized by academic and professional themes.
> Each word includes a definition and Traditional Chinese (繁體中文) translation.
> These 8000 words do NOT repeat the 1200 elementary-level words or the 3000 junior high school words.

---

## 1. Biology & Life Sciences

| # | Word | 中文 | Definition |
|---|------|------|------------|
| 1 | amoeba | 變形蟲 | A single-celled organism that moves by changing its shape |
| 2 | antibody | 抗體 | A protein produced by the immune system to fight specific pathogens |
| 3 | antigen | 抗原 | A foreign substance that triggers an immune response in the body |
| 4 | biochemistry | 生物化學 | The study of chemical processes within living organisms |
| 5 | bioethics | 生物倫理學 | The study of ethical issues arising from advances in biology and medicine |
| 6 | bioinformatics | 生物資訊學 | The use of computer science to analyze biological data |
| 7 | bioluminescence | 生物發光 | The production and emission of light by a living organism |
| 8 | biomass | 生物量 | The total mass of organisms in a given area or ecosystem |
| 9 | biosphere | 生物圈 | The global sum of all ecosystems where life exists |
| 10 | biotechnology | 生物技術 | The use of living systems to develop products and technologies |
| 11 | botany | 植物學 | The scientific study of plants |
| 12 | cartilage | 軟骨 | Firm, flexible connective tissue found in joints and other body parts |
| 13 | cell membrane | 細胞膜 | The thin layer surrounding a cell that controls what enters and exits |
| 14 | cell wall | 細胞壁 | A rigid outer layer found in plant cells that provides structural support |
| 15 | cellulose | 纖維素 | A complex carbohydrate that forms the main structural component of plant cell walls |
| 16 | chloroplast | 葉綠體 | The organelle in plant cells where photosynthesis takes place |
| 17 | circulatory | 循環的 | Relating to the system that moves blood through the body |
| 18 | coexist | 共存 | To live or exist together at the same time or in the same place |
| 19 | collagen | 膠原蛋白 | A structural protein found in skin, bones, and connective tissue |
| 20 | commensalism | 片利共生 | A relationship where one organism benefits and the other is unaffected |
| 21 | coniferous | 針葉的 | Relating to trees that bear cones and have needle-like leaves |
| 22 | deciduous | 落葉的 | Describing trees or shrubs that shed their leaves annually |
| 23 | decomposer | 分解者 | An organism that breaks down dead matter and recycles nutrients |
| 24 | deoxyribonucleic acid | 去氧核糖核酸 | The molecule (DNA) that carries genetic instructions for life |
| 25 | diaphragm | 橫膈膜 | The muscular membrane separating the chest and abdominal cavities |
| 26 | diffusion | 擴散 | The movement of molecules from high to low concentration |
| 27 | diploid | 二倍體 | A cell containing two complete sets of chromosomes |
| 28 | dominance | 顯性 | The condition where one allele masks the expression of another |
| 29 | dormancy | 休眠 | A period of inactivity in an organism to conserve energy |
| 30 | embryo | 胚胎 | An organism in the early stages of development before birth or hatching |
| 31 | endocrine | 內分泌的 | Relating to glands that secrete hormones directly into the bloodstream |
| 32 | endoplasmic reticulum | 內質網 | A network of membranes in a cell involved in protein and lipid synthesis |
| 33 | enzyme | 酵素 | A protein that speeds up chemical reactions in living organisms |
| 34 | epidermis | 表皮 | The outermost layer of cells covering an organism |
| 35 | epigenetics | 表觀遺傳學 | The study of changes in gene expression not caused by DNA sequence changes |
| 36 | estrogen | 雌激素 | A hormone responsible for female secondary sexual characteristics |
| 37 | eukaryote | 真核生物 | An organism whose cells contain a nucleus enclosed within a membrane |
| 38 | excretion | 排泄 | The process of removing metabolic waste products from the body |
| 39 | exoskeleton | 外骨骼 | A rigid external covering that provides support and protection |
| 40 | fermentation | 發酵 | An anaerobic process that converts sugars to acids, gases, or alcohol |
| 41 | fertilize | 使受精 | To join male and female reproductive cells to begin development |
| 42 | fibrous | 纖維的 | Consisting of or resembling fibers |
| 43 | fungi | 真菌 | A kingdom of organisms including mushrooms, yeasts, and molds |
| 44 | gamete | 配子 | A reproductive cell (sperm or egg) with half the normal chromosomes |
| 45 | gene expression | 基因表現 | The process by which information from a gene is used to make a product |
| 46 | gene therapy | 基因治療 | The treatment of disease by replacing or altering faulty genes |
| 47 | genetic engineering | 基因工程 | The direct manipulation of an organism's DNA to alter its characteristics |
| 48 | genome | 基因組 | The complete set of genetic material in an organism |
| 49 | genotype | 基因型 | The genetic makeup of an organism |
| 50 | genus | 屬 | A taxonomic rank grouping closely related species |
| 51 | gestation | 妊娠期 | The period of development inside the womb from conception to birth |
| 52 | gland | 腺體 | An organ that produces and releases substances for use in the body |
| 53 | glucose | 葡萄糖 | A simple sugar that is the primary source of energy for cells |
| 54 | glycogen | 肝醣 | A stored form of glucose found mainly in the liver and muscles |
| 55 | Golgi apparatus | 高爾基體 | An organelle that packages and distributes proteins within the cell |
| 56 | haploid | 單倍體 | A cell containing only one set of chromosomes |
| 57 | hemoglobin | 血紅素 | The protein in red blood cells that carries oxygen |
| 58 | heterotroph | 異營生物 | An organism that cannot produce its own food |

| 60 | homeostasis | 恆定性 | The maintenance of stable internal conditions in an organism |
| 61 | homologous | 同源的 | Having a similar structure due to shared ancestry |

| 63 | hormone | 荷爾蒙 | A chemical messenger produced by glands that regulates body functions |

| 66 | incubation | 孵化 | The process of keeping eggs warm for hatching or developing microbes |
| 67 | insulin | 胰島素 | A hormone that regulates blood sugar levels |
| 68 | invertebrate | 無脊椎動物 | An animal without a backbone |
| 69 | in vitro | 體外的 | Occurring in a laboratory setting rather than in a living organism |
| 70 | in vivo | 體內的 | Occurring within a living organism |
| 71 | keratin | 角蛋白 | A tough protein found in hair, nails, and outer skin layers |
| 72 | kingdom | 界 | The highest major taxonomic grouping of organisms |
| 73 | lactation | 泌乳 | The production and secretion of milk by mammary glands |
| 74 | larva | 幼蟲 | The immature form of an insect or animal before metamorphosis |

| 82 | melanin | 黑色素 | A pigment responsible for skin, hair, and eye color |
| 83 | meristem | 分生組織 | Plant tissue consisting of actively dividing cells for growth |
| 84 | metamorphosis | 變態 | A dramatic change in body form during an organism's development |
| 85 | microbiome | 微生物群系 | The community of microorganisms living in a particular environment |
| 86 | microorganism | 微生物 | A living thing too small to be seen without a microscope |
| 87 | mitochondria | 粒線體 | Organelles that generate most of the cell's energy supply |
| 88 | mitosis | 有絲分裂 | Cell division resulting in two identical daughter cells |
| 89 | molecular biology | 分子生物學 | The study of biology at the molecular level |
| 90 | monocot | 單子葉植物 | A flowering plant with one seed leaf |
| 91 | morphology | 形態學 | The study of the form and structure of organisms |
| 92 | mucous membrane | 黏膜 | The moist tissue lining body cavities and openings |
| 93 | multicellular | 多細胞的 | Consisting of many cells |
| 94 | mutualism | 互利共生 | A relationship where both organisms benefit from each other |
| 95 | natural selection | 天擇 | The process where organisms with favorable traits survive and reproduce |
| 96 | nerve | 神經 | A bundle of fibers that transmits impulses between the brain and body |
| 97 | neuron | 神經元 | A specialized cell that transmits nerve impulses |
| 98 | neurotransmitter | 神經傳導物質 | A chemical that transmits signals across nerve synapses |
| 99 | niche | 生態棲位 | The role and position an organism occupies in its ecosystem |
| 100 | nitrogen cycle | 氮循環 | The biogeochemical cycle by which nitrogen is converted in the environment |
| 101 | nucleic acid | 核酸 | A molecule (DNA or RNA) that carries genetic information |
| 102 | nucleotide | 核苷酸 | The basic structural unit of nucleic acids |
| 103 | organelle | 胞器 | A specialized structure within a cell that performs a specific function |
| 104 | osmosis | 滲透 | The movement of water through a membrane from low to high solute concentration |
| 105 | ovary | 卵巢 | The female reproductive organ that produces eggs |
| 106 | ovulation | 排卵 | The release of a mature egg from the ovary |
| 107 | paleontology | 古生物學 | The study of ancient life through fossils |
| 108 | pancreas | 胰臟 | An organ that produces insulin and digestive enzymes |
| 109 | parasitism | 寄生 | A relationship where one organism benefits while harming the host |
| 110 | pathogen | 病原體 | A microorganism that can cause disease |
| 111 | peptide | 肽 | A short chain of amino acids linked by peptide bonds |
| 112 | peristalsis | 蠕動 | Wave-like muscle contractions that move food through the digestive tract |
| 113 | permeable | 可滲透的 | Allowing substances to pass through |
| 114 | phagocyte | 吞噬細胞 | A cell that engulfs and digests foreign particles and pathogens |
| 115 | phenotype | 表現型 | The observable characteristics of an organism |
| 116 | phloem | 韌皮部 | Plant tissue that transports sugars from leaves to other parts |
| 117 | phylum | 門 | A major taxonomic division ranking below kingdom |
| 118 | physiology | 生理學 | The study of how living organisms and their parts function |
| 119 | pigment | 色素 | A substance that gives color to plant or animal tissue |
| 120 | pituitary gland | 腦下垂體 | A small gland at the base of the brain that controls other glands |

| 126 | polymerase | 聚合酶 | An enzyme that synthesizes long chains of nucleic acids |

| 128 | prokaryote | 原核生物 | An organism whose cells lack a membrane-bound nucleus |
| 129 | protist | 原生生物 | A eukaryotic organism that is not a plant, animal, or fungus |
| 130 | protozoa | 原生動物 | Single-celled organisms that can move and consume food |
| 131 | puberty | 青春期 | The stage of development when reproductive organs become functional |

| 134 | recessive | 隱性的 | An allele that is only expressed when two copies are present |

## 2. Chemistry

| # | Word | 中文 | Definition |
|---|------|------|------------|
| 205 | acid | 酸 | A substance that donates hydrogen ions and has a pH below 7 |
| 206 | activation energy | 活化能 | The minimum energy required for a chemical reaction to occur |
| 207 | alkali | 鹼 | A soluble base that produces hydroxide ions in solution |
| 208 | alkali metal | 鹼金屬 | A highly reactive metal in Group 1 of the periodic table |
| 209 | alkaline earth metal | 鹼土金屬 | A reactive metal in Group 2 of the periodic table |
| 210 | alkane | 烷類 | A saturated hydrocarbon with only single carbon-carbon bonds |
| 211 | alkene | 烯類 | An unsaturated hydrocarbon containing a carbon-carbon double bond |
| 212 | alkyne | 炔類 | An unsaturated hydrocarbon containing a carbon-carbon triple bond |
| 213 | allotrope | 同素異形體 | Different structural forms of the same element |
| 214 | alloy | 合金 | A mixture of metals or a metal combined with another element |
| 215 | amalgam | 汞齊 | An alloy containing mercury |
| 216 | amorphous | 非晶質的 | Lacking a definite crystalline structure |
| 217 | amphoteric | 兩性的 | Capable of acting as both an acid and a base |
| 218 | anhydrous | 無水的 | Containing no water molecules |
| 219 | anion | 陰離子 | A negatively charged ion |
| 220 | anode | 陽極 | The electrode where oxidation occurs |
| 221 | aqueous | 水溶液的 | Dissolved in water |
| 222 | aromatic | 芳香族的 | Relating to organic compounds containing a benzene ring structure |
| 223 | atomic mass | 原子量 | The weighted average mass of an atom of an element |
| 224 | atomic number | 原子序 | The number of protons in the nucleus of an atom |
| 225 | Avogadro's number | 亞佛加厥常數 | The number of particles in one mole of a substance (6.022 × 10²³) |
| 226 | base | 鹼 | A substance that accepts hydrogen ions and has a pH above 7 |
| 227 | boiling point | 沸點 | The temperature at which a liquid turns into a gas |
| 228 | bond energy | 鍵能 | The energy required to break a chemical bond |
| 229 | Brownian motion | 布朗運動 | The random movement of particles suspended in a fluid |
| 230 | buffer | 緩衝溶液 | A solution that resists changes in pH when small amounts of acid or base are added |
| 231 | burette | 滴定管 | A graduated glass tube used for dispensing precise volumes of liquid |
| 232 | by-product | 副產物 | A secondary product formed during a chemical reaction |
| 233 | calorimetry | 量熱法 | The measurement of heat changes in chemical reactions |
| 234 | cathode | 陰極 | The electrode where reduction occurs |
| 235 | cation | 陽離子 | A positively charged ion |
| 236 | centrifuge | 離心機 | A device that separates substances by spinning at high speed |
| 237 | chemical equation | 化學方程式 | A symbolic representation of a chemical reaction |
| 238 | chemical equilibrium | 化學平衡 | A state where the rates of forward and reverse reactions are equal |
| 239 | chemical reaction | 化學反應 | A process that transforms one set of substances into another |
| 240 | chromatography | 層析法 | A technique for separating mixtures based on different migration rates |
| 241 | coagulation | 凝聚 | The process of a liquid thickening into a semi-solid mass |
| 242 | colloid | 膠體 | A mixture with particles larger than a solution but smaller than a suspension |
| 243 | combustion | 燃燒 | A rapid chemical reaction with oxygen that produces heat and light |
| 244 | concentration | 濃度 | The amount of a substance dissolved in a given volume of solution |
| 245 | condensation | 凝結 | The change of a gas or vapor to a liquid |
| 246 | conductivity | 導電度 | The ability of a substance to conduct electric current |
| 247 | conjugate acid | 共軛酸 | The species formed when a base gains a proton |
| 248 | conjugate base | 共軛鹼 | The species formed when an acid donates a proton |
| 249 | corrosion | 腐蝕 | The gradual destruction of a material by chemical reaction with its environment |
| 250 | covalent bond | 共價鍵 | A chemical bond formed by sharing electrons between atoms |
| 251 | crystallize | 結晶 | To form crystals from a solution or melt |
| 252 | decomposition | 分解反應 | A reaction in which a compound breaks down into simpler substances |
| 253 | deliquescent | 潮解的 | Absorbing moisture from the air until dissolved |
| 254 | diatomic | 雙原子的 | Consisting of two atoms |
| 255 | dilute | 稀釋 | To reduce the concentration of a solution by adding solvent |
| 256 | displacement reaction | 置換反應 | A reaction where a more reactive element replaces a less reactive one |
| 257 | dissociation | 解離 | The separation of a compound into ions in solution |
| 258 | distillation | 蒸餾 | A process of separating liquids by differences in boiling points |
| 259 | double bond | 雙鍵 | A chemical bond involving two pairs of shared electrons |
| 260 | ductile | 可延展的 | Capable of being drawn into thin wires |
| 261 | effervescence | 起泡 | The formation of gas bubbles in a liquid during a chemical reaction |
| 262 | electrolysis | 電解 | Using electricity to drive a non-spontaneous chemical reaction |
| 263 | electrolyte | 電解質 | A substance that conducts electricity when dissolved in water |
| 264 | electron configuration | 電子組態 | The arrangement of electrons in the orbitals of an atom |
| 265 | electronegativity | 電負度 | The tendency of an atom to attract shared electrons |
| 266 | electroplating | 電鍍 | Coating a surface with metal using electrolysis |
| 267 | empirical formula | 實驗式 | The simplest whole-number ratio of atoms in a compound |
| 268 | emulsion | 乳化液 | A mixture of two immiscible liquids where one is dispersed in the other |
| 269 | endothermic | 吸熱的 | A reaction that absorbs heat from its surroundings |
| 270 | enthalpy | 焓 | The total heat content of a system at constant pressure |
| 271 | entropy | 熵 | A measure of disorder or randomness in a system |
| 272 | equilibrium constant | 平衡常數 | A value expressing the ratio of products to reactants at equilibrium |
| 273 | ester | 酯 | An organic compound formed from the reaction of an acid and an alcohol |
| 274 | ether | 醚 | An organic compound with an oxygen atom bonded to two carbon groups |
| 275 | exothermic | 放熱的 | A reaction that releases heat to its surroundings |
| 276 | extraction | 萃取 | The process of separating a substance from a mixture |
| 277 | fatty acid | 脂肪酸 | A long-chain carboxylic acid found in fats and oils |
| 278 | filtration | 過濾 | The process of separating solids from liquids using a filter |
| 279 | flammable | 易燃的 | Easily set on fire |
| 280 | free radical | 自由基 | An atom or molecule with an unpaired electron that is highly reactive |
| 281 | freezing point | 凝固點 | The temperature at which a liquid becomes a solid |
| 282 | functional group | 官能基 | A specific group of atoms responsible for the chemical properties of a molecule |
| 283 | galvanic cell | 伽凡尼電池 | An electrochemical cell that converts chemical energy into electrical energy |
| 284 | halogen | 鹵素 | A highly reactive nonmetal element in Group 17 of the periodic table |
| 285 | Hess's law | 乘斯定律 | The total enthalpy change of a reaction is the same regardless of the route |
| 286 | homogeneous | 均勻的 | Having uniform composition throughout |

## 5. Literature & Language Arts

| # | Word | 中文 | Definition |
|---|------|------|------------|
| 819 | allegory | 寓言；諷喻 | A story in which characters and events represent abstract ideas or moral qualities |
| 820 | allusion | 典故；引喻 | An indirect reference to a person, event, or work of literature |
| 821 | ambiguity | 模糊；歧義 | The quality of being open to more than one interpretation |
| 822 | archetype | 原型 | A typical example of a character, theme, or situation that recurs in literature |
| 823 | catharsis | 情感宣洩 | The release of strong emotions through art, especially tragedy |

| 826 | colloquial | 口語的 | Relating to informal, everyday spoken language |
| 827 | denouement | 結局 | The final part of a story in which conflicts are resolved |
| 828 | dystopia | 反烏托邦 | An imagined society characterized by suffering and oppression |
| 829 | elegy | 輓歌；哀詩 | A poem of mourning, usually for a deceased person |
| 830 | epigram | 警句；雋語 | A short, witty statement that conveys a truth or observation |
| 831 | epithet | 稱號；綽號 | A descriptive word or phrase used to characterize a person or thing |
| 832 | euphemism | 委婉語 | A mild expression used in place of one considered harsh or blunt |
| 833 | farce | 鬧劇 | A comic dramatic work using exaggerated situations and absurd events |
| 834 | foreshadow | 伏筆；預示 | To give hints or clues about what will happen later in a story |

## 9. Economics & Finance

| # | Word | 中文 | Definition |
|---|------|------|------------|

| 1800 | overvalued | 高估的 | Priced higher than the true or intrinsic value |

| 1803 | trade war | 貿易戰 | An economic conflict resulting from extreme protectionist measures |

## 22. Advanced Nouns - Abstract & Academic

| # | Word | 中文 | Definition |
|---|------|------|------------|
| 4291 | abstraction | 抽象概念 | a general idea that is not based on any particular real thing |
| 4292 | accumulation | 累積；積聚 | the gradual gathering of an increasing amount of something |
| 4293 | acknowledgment | 承認；致謝 | the act of accepting or recognizing something |
| 4294 | adaptation | 適應；改編 | the process of adjusting to new conditions or environment |
| 4295 | adherence | 遵守；堅持 | the act of following rules or sticking to beliefs |
| 4296 | adjunct | 附屬物；助手 | something added or attached in a supplementary way |
| 4297 | administration | 管理；行政 | the process of running a business or organization |
| 4298 | adversary | 對手；敵人 | a person or group that opposes or fights against another |
| 4299 | advocacy | 倡導；辯護 | public support for or recommendation of a cause |
| 4300 | affiliation | 隸屬關係 | a connection or association with an organization |
| 4301 | aftermath | 後果；餘波 | the consequences or aftereffects of a significant event |
| 4302 | allegiance | 忠誠；效忠 | loyalty or commitment to a leader, group, or cause |
| 4303 | allocation | 分配；配額 | the distribution of resources for a specific purpose |
| 4304 | altercation | 爭吵；口角 | a noisy argument or disagreement |

## 23. Advanced Adjectives & Modifiers

| # | Word | 中文 | Definition |
|---|------|------|------------|
| 4576 | aberrant | 異常的；偏差的 | departing from an accepted standard |
| 4577 | abject | 悲慘的；卑微的 | extremely bad, unpleasant, or degrading |
| 4578 | abrupt | 突然的；唐突的 | sudden and unexpected, or brief in manner |
| 4579 | absurd | 荒謬的；可笑的 | wildly unreasonable or illogical |
| 4580 | accessible | 易取得的；可接近的 | easily reached, entered, or understood |
| 4581 | acclaimed | 受讚譽的 | publicly praised and celebrated |
| 4582 | adamant | 堅決的；固執的 | refusing to be persuaded or to change one's mind |

## 24. Mathematics & Statistics

| # | Word | 中文 | Definition |
|---|------|------|------------|
| 4847 | abscissa | 橫坐標 | The horizontal coordinate of a point in a two-dimensional coordinate system |
| 4848 | absolute value | 絕對值 | The non-negative value of a number regardless of its sign |
| 4849 | amplitude | 振幅 | The maximum displacement of a periodic function from its equilibrium position |
| 4850 | asymptote | 漸近線 | A line that a curve approaches but never actually reaches |
| 4851 | axiom | 公理 | A statement accepted as true without proof, serving as a starting point for reasoning |
| 4852 | binomial | 二項式 | An algebraic expression consisting of two terms connected by addition or subtraction |
| 4853 | calculus | 微積分 | A branch of mathematics dealing with rates of change and accumulation of quantities |
| 4854 | cardinal number | 基數 | A number that indicates quantity, such as one, two, or three |
| 4855 | Cartesian | 笛卡兒的 | Relating to the coordinate system using perpendicular axes named after René Descartes |
| 4856 | collinear | 共線的 | Lying on the same straight line |
| 4857 | combinatorics | 組合數學 | The branch of mathematics dealing with counting, arrangement, and combination of objects |
| 4858 | commutative | 交換的 | A property where the order of operations does not affect the result |
| 4859 | complex number | 複數 | A number that has both a real part and an imaginary part |

| 5034 | corollary | 推論 | A proposition that follows directly from a proven theorem with little additional proof |

## 25. Academic Writing & Research

| # | Word | 中文 | Definition |
|---|------|------|------------|
| 5035 | accuracy | 準確性 | The degree to which a result conforms to the correct or true value |
| 5036 | addendum | 附錄補充 | Additional material added at the end of a document or publication |
| 5037 | affirmation | 肯定 | A positive declaration or confirmation of something as true |
| 5038 | ambiguity | 歧義 | The quality of being open to more than one interpretation |
| 5039 | annotation | 註解 | A note or comment added to a text to provide explanation or clarification |
| 5040 | anomaly | 異常 | Something that deviates from what is standard, normal, or expected |
| 5041 | apparatus | 儀器 | The technical equipment or tools needed for a particular experiment or activity |
| 5042 | appraisal | 評價 | A formal assessment or evaluation of something |
| 5043 | case study | 個案研究 | An in-depth analysis of a particular instance or event used for broader understanding |
| 5044 | caveat | 警告 | A warning or caution about potential limitations or problems |
| 5045 | clarification | 澄清 | The act of making a statement or situation clearer and easier to understand |
| 5046 | classification | 分類 | The systematic arrangement of items into categories based on shared characteristics |
| 5047 | collaboration | 合作 | The act of working jointly with others on an academic or research project |
| 5048 | colloquium | 學術研討會 | An academic seminar where scholars present and discuss their research |
| 5049 | compilation | 彙編 | A collection of items gathered together from various sources |
| 5050 | complement | 補充 | Something that completes or enhances another thing |
| 5051 | compliance | 遵守 | The act of conforming to rules, standards, or regulations |
| 5052 | component | 組成部分 | An essential part or element of a larger whole |
| 5053 | conceptual | 概念的 | Relating to abstract ideas or general notions |
| 5054 | conclusion | 結論 | The final section of a paper summarizing findings and implications |
| 5055 | concordance | 索引 | An alphabetical list of important words used in a text with references |
| 5056 | conference | 學術會議 | A formal meeting for discussion of research and academic topics |
| 5057 | confidentiality | 保密性 | The ethical principle of keeping research participants' information private |
| 5058 | confirmation | 確認 | Evidence or proof that supports a theory or finding |
| 5059 | consolidation | 整合 | The process of combining multiple sources or ideas into a unified whole |
| 5060 | contention | 論點 | A point argued in a debate or discussion |
| 5061 | contradiction | 矛盾 | A situation where two statements or ideas oppose each other |
| 5062 | contribution | 貢獻 | The part played by a person or work in bringing about a result or advancing knowledge |
| 5063 | convention | 慣例 | A widely accepted standard or practice in academic writing |
| 5064 | copyright | 著作權 | The legal right of an author to control reproduction of their work |
| 5065 | corroboration | 佐證 | Evidence that confirms or supports a statement or theory |
| 5066 | credibility | 可信度 | The quality of being trusted and believed in |
| 5067 | curriculum vitae | 履歷 | A detailed document outlining a person's academic and professional history |
| 5068 | deduction | 推論 | The process of reasoning from general premises to a specific conclusion |
| 5069 | definition | 定義 | A clear statement of the exact meaning of a word or concept |
| 5070 | deliberation | 審議 | Careful consideration and discussion before reaching a conclusion |
| 5071 | delineation | 描繪 | The detailed description or portrayal of something |
| 5072 | demographic | 人口統計的 | Relating to the statistical characteristics of a population |
| 5073 | derivation | 推導 | The process of developing a theory or formula from existing knowledge |
| 5074 | deviation | 偏差 | A departure from an established standard or expected value |
| 5075 | disclaimer | 免責聲明 | A statement denying responsibility or limiting the scope of claims |
| 5076 | disclosure | 揭露 | The act of making new or secret information known |
| 5077 | discovery | 發現 | The act of finding something new or previously unknown |
| 5078 | discrepancy | 差異 | A lack of consistency or agreement between facts or claims |
| 5079 | discussion | 討論 | The section of a paper that interprets and explains the results |
| 5080 | documentation | 文件記錄 | The written materials that provide evidence or proof of something |
| 5081 | elaboration | 闡述 | The process of developing an idea in greater detail |
| 5082 | elucidation | 闡明 | The act of making something clear by providing additional explanation |
| 5083 | empirical | 實證的 | Based on verifiable observation or experience rather than theory |
| 5084 | endorsement | 認可 | An expression of approval or support for a theory or finding |
| 5085 | enumeration | 列舉 | The act of listing items one by one in a systematic way |

| 5134 | specification | 規格說明 | A detailed description of requirements or standards |
| 5135 | statistical | 統計的 | Relating to the use of statistics in research |

| 5137 | submission | 投稿 | The act of presenting a paper or article for publication |
| 5138 | substantiation | 證實 | The act of providing evidence to support or prove a claim |
| 5139 | survey | 調查 | A method of gathering information by questioning a selected group |
| 5140 | symposium | 學術研討會 | A conference organized around a particular academic topic |
| 5141 | synopsis | 概要 | A brief summary or outline of a longer work |
| 5142 | taxonomy | 分類學 | The science of classification according to a system of categories |
| 5143 | terminology | 術語 | The specialized vocabulary used in a particular field of study |
| 5144 | textual | 文本的 | Relating to or based on a written text |
| 5145 | topic | 主題 | The subject matter of a piece of writing or discussion |
| 5146 | validity | 效度 | The degree to which a study accurately measures what it intends to measure |
| 5147 | verification | 驗證 | The process of establishing the truth or correctness of something |
| 5148 | corrigendum | 勘誤 | A correction to a published work noting errors |
| 5149 | coauthor | 共同作者 | A person who writes a publication jointly with one or more other authors |
| 5150 | plagiarize | 剽竊 | To take and use another's work or ideas as one's own without credit |
| 5151 | extrapolate | 推斷 | To extend findings or conclusions beyond the immediate data |
| 5152 | substantive | 實質的 | Having a firm basis in reality and therefore important or meaningful |
| 5153 | anecdotal | 軼事的 | Based on personal accounts rather than systematic research |
| 5154 | longitudinal | 縱貫的 | A study conducted over a long period observing the same subjects |

| 5175 | cohort | 世代群組 | A group of individuals sharing a common characteristic in a study |

| 5182 | errata | 勘誤表 | A list of errors and their corrections in a published work |

| 5184 | experimental group | 實驗組 | The group in an experiment that receives the treatment |
| 5185 | falsifiability | 可否證性 | The capacity of a hypothesis to be proven false through evidence |
| 5186 | field study | 田野研究 | Research conducted in a natural setting outside the laboratory |
| 5187 | grounded theory | 紮根理論 | A research methodology that develops theory from systematically gathered data |
| 5188 | informed consent | 知情同意 | Agreement to participate in research after understanding its nature and risks |
| 5189 | interpolate | 內插 | To estimate values between two known data points |

| 5191 | outlier | 離群值 | A data point that is significantly different from other observations |

| 5193 | pilot study | 先導研究 | A small preliminary study conducted to test research methods |

| 5197 | sampling bias | 抽樣偏差 | A systematic error caused by non-representative sample selection |
| 5198 | saturation | 飽和 | The point in qualitative research where new data no longer yields new insights |
| 5199 | spurious | 虛假的 | Apparently true but actually false or misleading in research |
| 5200 | stratification | 分層 | The division of a population into subgroups for sampling purposes |
| 5201 | theoretical | 理論的 | Based on or relating to theory rather than practice |
| 5202 | abstract noun | 抽象名詞 | A word that names an idea or quality rather than a physical object |
| 5203 | empiricism | 經驗主義 | The theory that knowledge comes primarily from sensory experience |
| 5204 | pragmatism | 實用主義 | A philosophical approach that evaluates ideas by their practical outcomes |
| 5205 | objectivity | 客觀性 | The quality of basing judgments on facts rather than personal feelings |
| 5206 | subjectivity | 主觀性 | The quality of basing judgments on personal feelings or opinions |
| 5207 | disseminate | 傳播 | To spread information or research findings widely |
| 5208 | elucidate | 闡明 | To make something clear through detailed explanation |
| 5209 | substantiate | 證實 | To provide evidence that supports or proves a claim |
| 5210 | delineate | 界定 | To describe or outline something precisely |

## 28. Environmental Science & Sustainability

| # | Word | 中文 | Definition |
|---|------|------|------------|
| 5588 | acidification | 酸化 | The process by which water or soil becomes more acidic, often due to pollution |
| 5589 | afforestation | 造林 | The process of planting trees on land that was not previously forested |
| 5590 | algal bloom | 藻華 | A rapid increase in the population of algae in a body of water, often harmful |

## 30. World Religions & Belief Systems

| # | Word | 中文 | Definition |
|---|------|------|------------|
| 5977 | agnosticism | 不可知論 | The belief that the existence of God cannot be known or proven |
| 5978 | altar | 祭壇 | A table or flat-topped structure used for religious offerings or rituals |
| 5979 | ancestor worship | 祖先崇拜 | The practice of honoring and praying to deceased family members |
| 5980 | angel | 天使 | A spiritual being believed to act as a messenger of God |

## 31. Formal & Academic Expressions

| # | Word | 中文 | Definition |
|---|------|------|------------|
| 6219 | above-mentioned | 上述的 | Referred to or discussed earlier in a text |
| 6220 | addendum | 附錄 | An additional item added at the end of a document |
| 6221 | admittedly | 公認地 | Used to introduce a concession or acknowledgment of a fact |
| 6222 | aforementioned | 前述的 | Mentioned earlier in the same text or discussion |
| 6223 | albeit | 儘管 | Although; even though |
| 6224 | as a consequence | 結果 | As a result of something |
| 6225 | as it stands | 就目前而言 | In its current state or condition |
| 6226 | as opposed to | 相對於 | In contrast with; rather than |
| 6227 | at the outset | 在開始時 | At the very beginning |
| 6228 | be that as it may | 儘管如此 | Despite what has just been said |
| 6229 | bearing in mind | 考慮到 | Taking into account; remembering |
| 6230 | broadly speaking | 概括而言 | In general terms; without going into detail |
| 6231 | by and large | 大體上 | On the whole; generally |
| 6232 | by the same token | 同樣地 | In the same way; for the same reason |
| 6233 | categorically | 斷然地 | In a way that is absolute and without exception |
| 6234 | circumstantial | 視情況的 | Based on circumstances rather than definite proof |
| 6235 | cognizant | 認知到的 | Fully aware or informed of something |
| 6236 | commensurate | 相稱的 | Corresponding in size, degree, or extent |
| 6237 | compellingly | 令人信服地 | In a way that evokes interest or admiration strongly |
| 6238 | concurrently | 同時地 | At the same time; simultaneously |
| 6239 | concomitant | 伴隨的 | Naturally accompanying or associated with something |
| 6240 | contingent upon | 取決於 | Dependent on certain conditions being met |
| 6241 | correspondingly | 相應地 | In a way that matches or relates to something else |
| 6242 | deem | 認為 | To regard or consider in a specified way |
| 6243 | discernibly | 明顯地 | In a way that can be perceived or recognized |
| 6244 | dispensation | 特許 | Exemption from a rule or usual requirement |
| 6245 | dissemination | 傳播 | The act of spreading information or knowledge widely |
| 6246 | due to the fact that | 由於 | Because; for the reason that |
| 6247 | elucidate | 闡釋 | To make something clear by providing more detail |
| 6248 | encompass | 包含 | To include or contain within a larger scope |
| 6249 | engender | 產生 | To cause or give rise to a feeling, situation, or condition |
| 6250 | erstwhile | 從前的 | Former; of a previous time |
| 6251 | exacerbate | 使惡化 | To make a problem, bad situation, or negative feeling worse |
| 6252 | existential | 存在主義的 | Relating to existence, especially human existence and its meaning |
| 6253 | extrinsic | 外在的 | Coming from outside; not part of the essential nature of something |
| 6254 | for the most part | 大多數情況下 | Usually; in most cases |
| 6255 | forthwith | 立即 | Immediately; without delay |
| 6256 | henceforth | 從此以後 | From this time on; from now on |
| 6257 | hitherto | 迄今為止 | Until now; up to this point in time |
| 6258 | hypothetically | 假設地 | In a way based on a possible situation rather than a real one |
| 6259 | inasmuch as | 因為；由於 | To the extent that; since |
| 6260 | incidentally | 順帶一提 | By the way; as a minor point |
| 6261 | insofar as | 在⋯範圍內 | To the extent that |
| 6262 | in the context of | 在⋯背景下 | With regard to the surrounding circumstances |
| 6263 | in the event that | 萬一 | If it should happen that |
| 6264 | in this regard | 在這方面 | Concerning this matter |
| 6265 | intrinsic | 內在的 | Belonging naturally; essential |
| 6266 | ipso facto | 根據事實本身 | By that very fact or act |
| 6267 | irrespective | 不論 | Regardless of; without taking something into account |
| 6268 | it follows that | 由此可得 | It is a logical consequence that |
| 6269 | juxtapose | 並列 | To place close together for comparison or contrast |
| 6270 | lest | 以免 | For fear that; in order to prevent |
| 6271 | manifestly | 明顯地 | In a way that is clear or obvious to see |
| 6272 | moot | 有爭議的 | Subject to debate; arguable; no longer relevant |
| 6273 | mutatis mutandis | 在細節作必要修改後 | With the necessary changes having been made |
| 6274 | notwithstanding | 儘管 | In spite of; nevertheless |
| 6275 | on the contrary | 相反地 | Used to introduce a statement that contradicts what was just said |
| 6276 | on the grounds that | 基於 | For the reason that; because |
